Ratio)</span></a></div><div><a class="flex items-center px-4 py-2.5 rounded-xl transition-colors duration-200 text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-400 hover:bg-gray-50/50 dark:hover:bg-gray-700/30" href="/zh/factors/value/dividend-rate"><span class="text-sm font-medium">股息收益率</span></a></div><div><a class="flex items-center px-4 py-2.5 rounded-xl transition-colors duration-200 text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-400 hover:bg-gray-50/50 dark:hover:bg-gray-700/30" href="/zh/factors/value/market-cap"><span class="text-sm font-medium">流通市值对数因子</span></a></div><div><a class="flex items-center px-4 bg-blue-50/50 dark:bg-blue-900/20 text-blue-600 dark:text-blue-400"><span>规模因子</span><span class="ml-auto" style="transform: rotate(90deg);"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" 6-6-6-6"></path></svg></span></button><div class="overflow-hidden" style="height: auto; opacity: 1;"><div class="pt-1 space-y-1"><div><a class="flex items-center px-4 py-2.5 rounded-xl dark:hover:bg-gray-700/30" href="/zh/factors/scale/free-float-market-cap"><span class="text-sm font-medium">自由流通市值</span></a></div><div><a class="flex items-center px-4 py-2.5 rounded-xl font-medium">对数市值规模</span></a></div></div></div></div></div></nav></div><main class="flex-1 px-2 py-4 sm:px-4 md:px-6 lg:px-8"><div lang="zh"><h1 class="sr-only">Factors Directory</h1><h2 class="sr-only">Quantitative Trading Factors</h2><article class="max-w-4xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 py-8" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><header class="mb-8"><h1 class="text-3xl font-medium mb-4">成交量价背离度</h1><div class="flex gap-2"><span class="inline-flex items-center px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-sm  bg-[#fbfbfb] text-[#232121] border border-[#393939]/10 hover:bg-[#393939]/5 transition-colors duration-200">技术因子</span></div></header><section class="mb-6 bg-white dark:bg-[#1A1A1A] rounded-2xl p-6 sm:p-8 shadow-sm"><h2 class="text-xl font-medium mb-4 flex items-center"><span class="mr-2">因子公式</span></h2><div class="mb-4"><p class="text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300 mb-2">成交量价背离度计算:</p><div class="overflow-x-auto bg-gray-50 dark:bg-gray-600/30 p-4 sm:p-6 rounded-xl shadow-inner"><div class="min-w-[300px] w-full flex items-center justify-center"><span class="__Latex__"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>C</mi><mi>O</mi><mi>R</mi><mi>R</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>V</mi><mi>W</mi><mi>A</mi><msub><mi>P</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>d</mi><mo>:</mo><mi>t</mi></mrow></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mi>O</mi><mi>L</mi><mi>U</mi><mi>M</mi><msub><mi>E</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>d</mi><mo>:</mo><mi>t</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex"> CORR(VWAP_{t-d:t}, VOLUME_{t-d:t}) </annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">CORR</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">VW</span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">d</span><span class="mrel mtight">:</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2083em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.02778em;">O</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.10903em;">LU</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">E</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0576em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">d</span><span class="mrel mtight">:</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2083em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></div></div></div><div class="mt-6"><p class="text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300 mb-3">公式中:</p><ul class="space-y-2"><li class="flex items-center text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300"><div class="mr-3"><span class="__Latex__"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>C</mi><mi>O</mi><mi>R</mi><mi>R</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">CORR</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">CORR</span></span></span></span></span></div><span class="mr-1">:</span><div class="ml-3"><p>表示皮尔逊相关系数 (Pearson Correlation Coefficient)，用于衡量两个变量之间的线性相关性强度。其值介于 -1 和 1 之间，-1表示完全负相关，1表示完全正相关，0表示无线性相关性。</p></div></li><li class="flex items-center text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300"><div class="mr-3"><span class="__Latex__"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>V</mi><mi>W</mi><mi>A</mi><msub><mi>P</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>d</mi><mo>:</mo><mi>t</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">VWAP_{t-d:t}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8917em;vertical-align:-0.2083em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">VW</span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">d</span><span class="mrel mtight">:</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2083em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div><span class="mr-1">:</span><div class="ml-3"><p>表示从 t-d 时刻到 t 时刻的成交量加权平均价格 (Volume Weighted Average Price) 时间序列。VWAP能够体现该时间段内的平均交易成本，能有效平滑短期价格波动。其中，t代表当前时间点，d代表回溯时间窗口的长度（如10天、20天）。</p></div></li><li class="flex items-center text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300"><div class="mr-3"><span class="__Latex__"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>V</mi><mi>O</mi><mi>L</mi><mi>U</mi><mi>M</mi><msub><mi>E</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>d</mi><mo>:</mo><mi>t</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">VOLUME_{t-d:t}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8917em;vertical-align:-0.2083em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.02778em;">O</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.10903em;">LU</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">E</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0576em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">d</span><span class="mrel mtight">:</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2083em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div><span class="mr-1">:</span><div class="ml-3"><p>表示从 t-d 时刻到 t 时刻的成交量时间序列，反映了该时间段内的市场活跃程度。成交量是市场情绪和参与程度的重要指标，其变动往往领先于价格。</p></div></li></ul></div></section><section class="mb-6 bg-white dark:bg-[#1A1A1A] rounded-2xl p-6 sm:p-8 shadow-sm"><h2 class="text-xl font-medium mb-4">因子解释</h2><div class="prose prose-gray dark:prose-invert max-w-none"><p>成交量价背离度通过计算在指定时间窗口内，成交量加权平均价格 (VWAP) 时间序列和成交量 (VOLUME) 时间序列之间的皮尔逊相关系数来量化价格与成交量背离的程度。该相关系数为正值时，表示价格与成交量同向变化，市场动能较强；而负值则表示价格与成交量反向变化，出现背离现象。例如，当价格持续上涨但成交量下降时，相关系数为负，表明价格上涨可能缺乏成交量的支撑，存在“冷场”现象，预示价格上涨动能可能减弱或潜在的回调风险。投资者可以利用该指标结合其他技术分析工具，如趋势线、支撑阻力位等，辅助判断市场趋势的可靠性和潜在的风险，尤其是在市场反转信号的识别中具有一定参考意义。需要注意的是，该指标不应单独使用，应结合市场整体环境和个股具体情况进行综合分析。</p></div></section><div class="mb-6 bg-gradient-to-r from-red-50 to-amber-50 dark:from-red-900/20 dark:to-amber-900/20 border border-red-200 dark:border-red-800 rounded-xl p-4" role="alert"><div class="flex items-start gap-3"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke-width="1.5" stroke="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" data-slot="icon" class="h-6 w-6 text-red-600 dark:text-red-400 flex-shrink-0 mt-0.5"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M12 9v3.75m-9.303 3.376c-.866 1.5.217 3.374 1.948 3.374h14.71c1.73 0 2.813-1.874 1.948-3.374L13.949 3.378c-.866-1.5-3.032-1.5-3.898 0L2.697 16.126ZM12 15.75h.007v.008H12v-.008Z"></path></svg><div class="space-y-2"><p class="text-sm font-semibold text-red-800 dark:text-red-300">⚠️ 因子风险警告</p><p class="text-sm text-red-700 dark:text-red-400">本量化因子仅供教育和研究目的使用。历史表现不保证未来收益。用户须独立验证并承担所有风险。</p></div></div></div><section class="mt-12 bg-white/50 dark:bg-[#1A1A1A]/50 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-2xl p-6 Divergence Degree）是一种衡量价格与成交量之间背离程度的技术分析指标。当价格（如股票价格或指数）的变动方向与成交量的变动方向不一致时，即出现背离。该指标旨在量化这种背离现象的强度，从而辅助判断市场趋势的潜在风险和动能。\",\"explanation\":\"成交量价背离度通过计算在指定时间窗口内，成交量加权平均价格 (VWAP) 时间序列和成交量 (VOLUME) 时间序列之间的皮尔逊相关系数来量化价格与成交量背离的程度。该相关系数为正值时，表示价格与成交量同向变化，市场动能较强；而负值则表示价格与成交量反向变化，出现背离现象。例如，当价格持续上涨但成交量下降时，相关系数为负，表明价格上涨可能缺乏成交量的支撑，存在“冷场”现象，预示价格上涨动能可能减弱或潜在的回调风险。投资者可以利用该指标结合其他技术分析工具，如趋势线、支撑阻力位等，辅助判断市场趋势的可靠性和潜在的风险，尤其是在市场反转信号的识别中具有一定参考意义。需要注意的是，该指标不应单独使用，应结合市场整体环境和个股具体情况进行综合分析。\",\"name\":\"成交量价背离度\",\"title\":\"成交量价背离度\",\"tags\":[\"技术因子\"],\"formulas\":[{\"text\":\"成交量价背离度计算:\",\"latex\":\"CORR(VWAP_{t-d:t}, 之间，-1表示完全负相关，1表示完全正相关，0表示无线性相关性。\"},{\"symbol\":\"VWAP_{t-d:t}\",\"meaning\":\"表示从 t-d 时刻到 t 时刻的成交量加权平均价格 (Volume Weighted Average Price) 时间序列。VWAP能够体现该时间段内的平均交易成本，能有效平滑短期价格波动。其中，t代表当前时间点，d代表回溯时间窗口的长度（如10天、20天）。\"},{\"symbol\":\"VOLUME_{t-d:t}\",\"meaning\":\"表示从 t-d 时刻到 t 时刻的成交量时间序列，反映了该时间段内的市场活跃程度。成交量是市场情绪和参与程度的重要指标，其变动往往领先于价格。\"}]},\"references\":[],\"related\":[{\"categoryId\":\"volatility\",\"factorId\":\"volatility-coefficient-of-turnover\",\"factorName\":\"成交额变异系数\"},{\"categoryId\":\"tech\",\"factorId\":\"volume-moving-average-convergence-divergence\",\"factorName\":\"成交量异同移动平均线
